Corsaros is possibly my favorite place for pizza! It is quite a drive from where we live, but whenever we are in the area, it is always on the top of our list of restaurants to go to. The pizzas are a bit pricey, but this is a family run restaurant that provides great food, so it kind of evens out. If you go, you absolutely have to have the breadsticks!!! I'm not a fan of pepperoni in general, but their vegetarian pizza is top-notch and loaded with delicious veggies. My parents get pepperoni and they say it's very good, too. As far as COVID,  I haven't been inside the restaurant but my parents have. The staff are friendly, wearing masks, and cleaning any surfaces you touch as soon as you're done, and pickup is a breeze. There's a nice area with some benches and beautiful plants as well as string lights on the same street where you can eat if you want to.<//text>
